 is list main amit shah kaa bhi naam he or yah saat march kii subah 10:55 baje kaa he

 dilachasp he ki yah phone kol ipel-4 main do nai tiimon ko shaamil karne ke baad shuru huevivadke duusare din kaa he

 bihar chunaav main lagbhag maheene bhar kaa vakt bachaa he 
 
 
 Ideally, everything should have been decided by now, but it is not so for the NDA
 chunavi aanch par muddon kii handi to chadha di gai he lekin abhi yahi nahin tay ho paaya he ki pakegaa kya or handi main kya kitna dalegaa
 
 
 That means BJP and its allies have neither been able to decide the name of the CM candidate, nor who will contest on how many seats
 ab sawaal he ki aakhir aisa kyon he
 To understand this, you have to understand the Dalit factor of Bihar election
 
 
 or saath hi yah samajhnaa hoga ki kya mahadalit mahajit kii vajah ban saktaa he? Consider the Dalit factor of the first Bihar election
 bihar kii kul aabaadi main 15
 9% are Dalits
 or rajya main 18
 44% of the voters are Dalits
 yani saare dalit vot ko mila den to kamobesh yadav vot bank kii barabari kaa maamla ban jaataa he
 In this too, 70% of the vote of SC quota is of Ravidas, Mushar and Paswan caste
 yani ek prabhavi vot bank
 If the RJD, Congress and JDU are considering the Kurmi, Muslim and Yadav vote banks in Bihar as their share, then the BJP is betting on the votes of the forward castes and the business class
 aise main soobe main dalit vot bank satta kii disha or dasha donon tay kar saktaa he is baar
 By the way, the Dalit seeks his Messiah in almost every election
 pehle congress par bharosa kiya, vahaan munh kii khai to lalu yadav kii argedy kaa daaman thama
 If not much was found there, then turned to Nitish Kumar's JDU
 nitish kumaar ne bhi SC category kii 22 jatiyon main se 21 ko mahadalit ghoshit kar apni taraf se koshishen shuru kin lekin unke raste main unka hi pyaadaa aa khadaa hua
 Manjhi kept his focus more or less on how he could become the face of Mahadalit during his tenure of about 8 months
 isi koshish ke tahat unhone kursi se hatate hatate bhi kai faisle mahadaliton ke haq main liye or paswan jati ko bhi mahadalit kii list main shaamil kar diya
 In such a situation, the fight became interesting this time
 bijepi na sirf maanjhi ko saath lekar ek dalit chehre ko sammaan dene kii baat kar rahi he balki maanjhi se kursi chhine jane ko bhi dalit ke apmaan kaa mudda bana rahi he
 Meanwhile, the problem for the BJP is that it has to decide who will bring more Dalit votes for it, Ram Vilas Paswan or Jeetan Ram Manjhi
 bijepi kii yah duvidha kyon he ise samajhane ke liye ek or aankada aapke saamne rakhte hai
 
 
 There are 38 total reserved seats in Bihar Legislative Assembly
 isamen se 2005 main JDU ko 15 siten mili thim or 2010 main 19 siten
 Remember that Manjhi was with JDU in these elections
 ab BJP kaa hisaab kitaab dekh lijie
 BJP had won 12 seats in 2005 and 18 in 2010, i
e
 the NDA alliance won 37 out of 38 seats in the last election
 RJD ko 2005 main 6 siten mili thim jo 2010 main ghatakar ek rah gai thi
 The LJP, which won 2 seats in 2005, did not even open an account on these seats in 2010 and the Congress was in a similar situation
 yani sidhe-sidhe hisaab yah he ki bijepi ke paas yah tay karne ke liye koi aankada nahin he ki JDU se alag hone ke baad jithan ram maanjhi kitna bada cheharaa ban gaye hai dalit vot bank ke liye or kya ramvilas paswan lalu yadav se alag hokar apana paaramparik paswan vot bank phir se hasil kar paaenge
 However, remember also that the other coalition also has to decide what it has to influence the Dalit vote bank
 isko agar chehron ke lihaaj se samajhie to tasviir aisi dikhegi
 
 tippaniyan LJP has the face of Ram Vilas Paswan who 4
 5% paswan vot par pakad kaa daawa karte hai
 Manjhi's Hindustani Awam Morcha i
e
 'hum' has only the support of Jeetan Ram Manjhi because he is 5
 5% musahar jati ke vot par asar daal sakate hai
 Apart from this, the ruling JDU also has many Dalit faces
 halaki nitish kumaar dalit cheharaa to nahin hai lekin daliton ke liye bahut kuch karne kaa daawa karke vot maangate rahe hai
 Apart from him, the party has Uday Narayan Chaudhary, Minister Shyam Rajak and another face of Ramai Ram
 dikkat sirf itani he ki is baar ke bihar ke chunaav main kai chehre jo saath the ve ab saath nahin hai or kai chehre jo saath nahin the ve ab saath hai
 The truth is that everyone talks about a place for the Dalit in the heart, but the Dalit can never get what he wants
 1994 se 2000 ke bich takreeban 144 log maare gaye, jinamein mahilaayein or bachche tak the
 These were the years when Lalu Yadav's party was in power
 lalu kuch nahin kar paae
 When Nitish came to power in 2005, he first abolished the slave commission, which was set up to investigate these killings
 sabake apane siyaasi daayre hai or raajnneetik jaruratein
 In such a situation, Dalit voters are now politically more mature than before
 vah khud bhi apane hisaab se satta kii gaadi chalaane kii ummiden paale he or isliye is baar yah prabhavi dalit vot bank kiske hisse jayega yah abhi kahana mushkil he
 That is, it is not decided whose face the voter will sit in the heart and whose face will show the mirror, but it is certain that the Dalit voter will play an important role in this Bihar election
 pehle bihar chunaav kaa dalit factor samajhie
 15 in Bihar's total population
 9% dalit hai
 And 18 in the state
 44% voter dalit hai
 That means, if all the Dalit votes are merged, then more or less Yadav becomes a matter of equality of vote bank
 isamen bhi SC cote ke vot kaa 70% hissaa ravidaas, musahar or paswan jati kaa he
 That is, an effective vote bank
 bihar main kurmi, musalmaan or yadav vot bank ko agar argedy, congress or jediu apane hisse main maan kar chal rahe hai to bijepi agadi jatiyon or vyapaaree varg ke vot par daanv lagaae baithi he
 In such a situation, the Dalit vote bank can decide both the direction and condition of power this time
 vaise to dalit lagbhag har chunaav main apana maseehaa talashta he
 Trusted the Congress first, there was a gap in the mouth, then Lalu Yadav joined the RJD
 vahaan bhi bahut kuch nahin mila to nitish kumaar kii jediu kaa rukh kiya
 Nitish Kumar also started efforts on his behalf by declaring 21 out of 22 castes of SC category as Mahadalit, but his pawn stood in his way
 maanjhi ne lagbhag 8 maheene ke kaarykaal main apana sara focus kamobesh is baat par rakhaa ki vah kaise mahadalit kaa cheharaa ban sake
 In the same effort, while moving away from the chair, he took many decisions in favor of Mahadalits and also included Paswan caste in the list of Mahadalits
 aise main is baar ladaai dilachasp ho gai
 BJP is not only talking about honoring a Dalit face by taking Manjhi along but also making Manjhi take away the chair, making it a point of insult to Dalit
 is bich bijepi ke liye dikkat yah he ki use tay karnaa he ki uske liye dalit vot zyada koun laaegaa, ramvilas paswan yaa jithan ram maanjhi
 To explain why BJP has this dilemma, let's put another figure in front of you
 
 
 bihar vidhansabha main kul arakshit siten 38 hai
 Of this, JDU got 15 seats in 2005 and 19 seats in 2010
 yah yaad rakhiegaa ki in chunaavon main maanjhi JDU ke saath the
 Now check the account of BJP
 BJP ke khate main 2005 main 12 siten ain thim or 2010 main 18, yani NDA gathbandhan ne pichley chunaav main 38 main se 37 siten jiti thim
 The RJD had got 6 seats in 2005 which was reduced to one in 2010
 2005 main 2 seat jeetne vaali LJP ne to 2010 main in siton par khaataa tak nahin kholaa or congress kaa bhi yahi haal tha
 This means that the BJP has no data to decide how big Jitan Ram Manjhi has become for the Dalit vote bank after separating from the JDU and whether Ram Vilas Paswan is separated from Lalu Yadav Will be able to regain his traditional Paswan vote bank
 halaki is bich yah bhi yaad rakhie ki duusare gathbandhan ko bhi yah tay karnaa he ki dalit vot bank ko prabhavit karne ke liye uske paas kya he
 If you consider it in terms of faces, the picture will look like this
 
 The comments LJP ke paas ramvilas paswan kaa cheharaa he jo 4
 5% Paswan claims a hold on the vote
 maanjhi ji kaa hindustani awam morcha yani 'ham' ke paas sirf jithan ram maanjhi kaa hi aasraa he kyonki vah 5
 5% of Mushars can influence the caste vote
 iske alaava sattarudh JDU main bhi kai dalit chehre hai
 Although Nitish Kumar is not a Dalit face, he has been demanding votes by claiming to do a lot for the Dalits
 unke alaava party main udai narayan choudhary hai, mantri shyaam rajak hai or ek or cheharaa ramai ram kaa he
 The only problem is that in the Bihar elections this time, many faces who were not together are no longer together and many faces who were not together are now together
 sach yah bhi he ki dil main dalit ke liye jagah kii baat to sab karte hai lekin dalit ko vah kabhi nahin mil paata jo uski chaah hoti he
 Some 144 people died between 1994 and 2000, including women and children
 yah saal aise the jab lalu yadav kii party satta main thi
 Lalu could not do anything
 nitish 2005 main satta main aae to sabase pehle us das kamishan ko bina report liye khatm kar diya, jo in hatyaon kii jaanch ke liye bani thi
 Everyone has their political circle and political needs
 aise main dalit voter bhi ab raajnneetik taur par pehle se zyada paripakv he
 He himself has raised hopes of running the power train according to his own and therefore this time it will be difficult to say to whom this effective Dalit vote bank will go
 yani tay nahin he ki voter kiske chehre ko dil main baithayega or kiske chehre ko aainaa dikhayega, lekin itnaa tay he ki dalit voter ahm kirdaar to nibhaayega is bihar chunaav main
